### CUT

- `P.1`
  Equation:

  \[X_{\mathrm{P_1}}^+ = A_{\mathrm{P_1}} X_{\mathrm{P_1}}^-, \qquad A_{\mathrm{P_1}} = T_{\mathrm{CUT}}^{-1} \Phi_{\mathrm{P_1}}^{\mathrm{AQM}} T_{\mathrm{CUT}}\]

  Variable legend: `X=(kappa,varphi,ell,b)` with containment, phase, liquid flux, and boundary integrity.
  Reading: extraction circuit / circulation circuit / valve control line.
  Confidence: mixed

### Aetheric

- `P.1`
  Equation:

  \[X_{\mathrm{P_1}}^+ = \mathrm{Expand}(g_{\mathrm{P_1}}^-) \oplus r_{\mathrm{P_1}}, \qquad g_{\mathrm{P_1}}^+ = \mathrm{Coll}(X_{\mathrm{P_1}}^+)\]

  Variable legend: `g` compressed seed, `X` expanded state, `r_line` residual address.

### Game Theory

- `P.1`
  Equation:

  \[y_{\mathrm{P_1}}^+ = \operatorname*{argmin}_{y \in \Delta(\mathcal{A})}\{R_{\mathrm{P_1}}(y) + \lambda_{\mathrm{P_1}} C(y, y_{\mathrm{P_1}}^-)\}\]

  Variable legend: `y` is the strategy distribution; `R_line` is risk and `C` the control-cost.
  Reading: extraction circuit / circulation circuit / valve control line.
  Confidence: mixed
